# Stack Protection Mechanisms in LLVM

## Your Task

Find all C++ source files in `llvm/llvm-project` that implement stack protection mechanisms against buffer overflow attacks. Specifically identify: 1. The LLVM pass that inserts stack protector checks (look for `StackProtector` in `llvm/lib/CodeGen/`). 2. The file that defines the `SafeStack` pass that separates safe and unsafe stack allocations (under `llvm/lib/CodeGen/`). 3. The header file that declares the stack protection pass interface. 4. The compiler-rt runtime file that provides the `__stack_chk_fail` implementation (look under `compiler-rt/lib/builtins/`). 5. Any file in `llvm/lib/Transforms/Instrumentation/` that implements memory safety instrumentation related to stack frame protection. Report the repo, file path, and the primary function or class handling stack protection for each.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the security domain.

## Available Resources

No local repositories are pre-checked out.

**Note:** Additional repositories are accessible via Sourcegraph MCP tools:
- `github.com/llvm/llvm-project` (llvm/llvm-project)
- `github.com/gcc-mirror/gcc` (gcc-mirror/gcc)

## Output Format

Create a file at `/workspace/answer.json` with your findings in the following structure:

```json
{
  "files": [
    {"repo": "org/repo-name", "path": "relative/path/to/file.go"}

}
```

Include only the fields relevant to this task. Your answer is evaluated against a closed-world oracle — completeness matters.

Perfect! I've successfully identified and documented all the C++ source files implementing stack protection mechanisms in LLVM. Here's a summary of what was found:

## Key Findings:

**Stack Protection Implementation Components:**

1. **StackProtector Pass** (`llvm/lib/CodeGen/StackProtector.cpp`)
   - Main LLVM pass inserting stack protector canaries
   - Classes: `StackProtector`, `StackProtectorPass`, `SSPLayoutAnalysis`
   - Key functions: `InsertStackProtectors()`, `CreateFailBB()`

2. **Stack Protector Interface** (`llvm/include/llvm/CodeGen/StackProtector.h`)
   - Declares `StackProtectorPass` and `StackProtector` classes
   - Defines `SSPLayoutAnalysis` for determining protection requirements

3. **SafeStack Pass** (`llvm/lib/CodeGen/SafeStack.cpp`)
   - Partitions stack into safe and unsafe regions
   - Main class: `SafeStack`, `SafeStackLegacyPass`
   - Separates vulnerable allocations to protected memory

4. **SafeStack Interface** (`llvm/include/llvm/CodeGen/SafeStack.h`)
   - Declares `SafeStackPass` for the new PassManager

5. **SafeStack Layout** (`llvm/lib/CodeGen/SafeStackLayout.cpp/h`)
   - Manages frame layout for stack objects
   - Classes: `StackLayout`
   - Functions: `layoutObject()`, `addObject()`

6. **Runtime Stack Check Handler** (`libc/src/compiler/generic/__stack_chk_fail.cpp`)
   - Implements `__stack_chk_fail()` - called on stack corruption
   - Defines `__stack_chk_guard` - random guard value

7. **Bounds Checking Instrumentation** (`llvm/lib/Transforms/Instrumentation/BoundsChecking.cpp`)
   - Provides additional memory safety checks
   - Class: `BoundsCheckingPass`
   - Functions: `getBoundsCheckCond()`, `addBoundsChecking()`

components that work together to detect and prevent stack buffer overflow attacks:\\n\\n## 1. Stack Protector Pass (llvm/lib/CodeGen/StackProtector.cpp)\\nThe main LLVM pass that inserts stack protectors into functions. The `StackProtector` class is a `FunctionPass` that:\\n- Detects functions requiring stack protection based on -fstack-protector flags\\n- Inserts stack guard values before local variables\\n- Inserts verification checks in epilogues that call `__stack_chk_fail()` if corruption is detected\\n- Key function: `InsertStackProtectors()` - implements prologue/epilogue insertion logic\\n- Key function: `CreateFailBB()` - creates the failure basic block with call to __stack_chk_fail\\n\\n## 2. Stack Protector Interface (llvm/include/llvm/CodeGen/StackProtector.h)\\nDefines the public interface for stack protection:\\n- `StackProtectorPass` - Modern pass interface using PassManager\\n- `StackProtector` - Legacy FunctionPass interface\\n- `SSPLayoutAnalysis` - Analyzes which variables trigger stack protection requirements\\n- `SSPLayoutInfo` - Stores layout information for protected stack objects\\n\\n## 3. SafeStack Pass (llvm/lib/CodeGen/SafeStack.cpp)\\nImplements the SafeStack security feature that partitions the stack into safe and unsafe regions:\\n- `SafeStack` class - main implementation for separating stack allocations\\n- `SafeStackLegacyPass` - legacy pass interface\\n- Separates allocations that are proven safe from those that could be vulnerable\\n- Unsafe allocations are moved to dynamically allocated unsafe stack managed by runtime library\\n- Includes stack protector checks for unsafe stack allocations\\n\\n## 4. SafeStack Interface (llvm/include/llvm/CodeGen/SafeStack.h)\\nDeclarates the public interface:\\n- `SafeStackPass` - Modern new-PM compatible pass interface\\n- Processes functions with SafeStack attribute\\n\\n## 5. SafeStack Layout (llvm/lib/CodeGen/SafeStackLayout.cpp/h)\\nManages frame layout for safe and unsafe stacks:\\n- `StackLayout` class - organizes stack objects with coloring and alignment\\n- `layoutObject()` - places stack objects efficiently in memory\\n- `addObject()` - registers new stack objects\\n- Ensures proper separation and alignment of stack allocations\\n\\n## 6. Stack Check Failure Handler (libc/src/compiler/generic/__stack_chk_fail.cpp)\\nRuntime implementation of the stack protection library function:\\n- `__stack_chk_fail()` - called when stack corruption is detected, prints \\\"stack smashing detected\\\\n\\\" and aborts\\n- `__stack_chk_guard` - global variable containing the random guard value (initialized to 0xa9fff01234)\\n- Located in LLVM libc's compiler support library\\n\\n## 7. Bounds Checking Instrumentation (llvm/lib/Transforms/Instrumentation/BoundsChecking.cpp)\\nProvides additional memory safety instrumentation for bounds checking:\\n- `BoundsCheckingPass` - detects and instruments out-of-bounds memory access operations\\n- `getBoundsCheckCond()` - determines conditions under which memory access will overflow\\n- `addBoundsChecking()` - inserts checks before load/store instructions\\n- Complements stack protectors with checks for heap and other memory regions\\n- Header at llvm/include/llvm/Transforms/Instrumentation/BoundsChecking.h\\n\\nTogether, these components provide defense-in-depth against stack buffer overflow attacks: StackProtector adds canary checks, SafeStack separates unsafe allocations to protected memory, and BoundsChecking instruments memory accesses to detect violations at runtime.\"\n}\n",

components that work together to detect and prevent stack buffer overflow attacks:\\n\\n## 1. Stack Protector Pass (llvm/lib/CodeGen/StackProtector.cpp)\\nThe main LLVM pass that inserts stack protectors into functions. The `StackProtector` class is a `FunctionPass` that:\\n- Detects functions requiring stack protection based on -fstack-protector flags\\n- Inserts stack guard values before local variables\\n- Inserts verification checks in epilogues that call `__stack_chk_fail()` if corruption is detected\\n- Key function: `InsertStackProtectors()` - implements prologue/epilogue insertion logic\\n- Key function: `CreateFailBB()` - creates the failure basic block with call to __stack_chk_fail\\n\\n## 2. Stack Protector Interface (llvm/include/llvm/CodeGen/StackProtector.h)\\nDefines the public interface for stack protection:\\n- `StackProtectorPass` - Modern pass interface using PassManager\\n- `StackProtector` - Legacy FunctionPass interface\\n- `SSPLayoutAnalysis` - Analyzes which variables trigger stack protection requirements\\n- `SSPLayoutInfo` - Stores layout information for protected stack objects\\n\\n## 3. SafeStack Pass (llvm/lib/CodeGen/SafeStack.cpp)\\nImplements the SafeStack security feature that partitions the stack into safe and unsafe regions:\\n- `SafeStack` class - main implementation for separating stack allocations\\n- `SafeStackLegacyPass` - legacy pass interface\\n- Separates allocations that are proven safe from those that could be vulnerable\\n- Unsafe allocations are moved to dynamically allocated unsafe stack managed by runtime library\\n- Includes stack protector checks for unsafe stack allocations\\n\\n## 4. SafeStack Interface (llvm/include/llvm/CodeGen/SafeStack.h)\\nDeclarates the public interface:\\n- `SafeStackPass` - Modern new-PM compatible pass interface\\n- Processes functions with SafeStack attribute\\n\\n## 5. SafeStack Layout (llvm/lib/CodeGen/SafeStackLayout.cpp/h)\\nManages frame layout for safe and unsafe stacks:\\n- `StackLayout` class - organizes stack objects with coloring and alignment\\n- `layoutObject()` - places stack objects efficiently in memory\\n- `addObject()` - registers new stack objects\\n- Ensures proper separation and alignment of stack allocations\\n\\n## 6. Stack Check Failure Handler (libc/src/compiler/generic/__stack_chk_fail.cpp)\\nRuntime implementation of the stack protection library function:\\n- `__stack_chk_fail()` - called when stack corruption is detected, prints \\\"stack smashing detected\\\\n\\\" and aborts\\n- `__stack_chk_guard` - global variable containing the random guard value (initialized to 0xa9fff01234)\\n- Located in LLVM libc's compiler support library\\n\\n## 7. Bounds Checking Instrumentation (llvm/lib/Transforms/Instrumentation/BoundsChecking.cpp)\\nProvides additional memory safety instrumentation for bounds checking:\\n- `BoundsCheckingPass` - detects and instruments out-of-bounds memory access operations\\n- `getBoundsCheckCond()` - determines conditions under which memory access will overflow\\n- `addBoundsChecking()` - inserts checks before load/store instructions\\n- Complements stack protectors with checks for heap and other memory regions\\n- Header at llvm/include/llvm/Transforms/Instrumentation/BoundsChecking.h\\n\\nTogether, these components provide defense-in-depth against stack buffer overflow attacks: StackProtector adds canary checks, SafeStack separates unsafe allocations to protected memory, and BoundsChecking instruments memory accesses to detect violations at runtime.\"\n}\n",
